# Division template historical names system. Is a new method of naming the divisions based on the names-group assigned to it's template.
# If we run out of all historical names, the names will be assigned in the old way.
#
# Each group has a made up tag. Use it if you want to append more, or replace existing names with the extra txt files (modding).
#
# for_countries - lists all countries that can use it. If empty, or entire tag is missing, all countries in the world can use it.
#
# can_use - is a trigger that locks/unlocks the group under specific circumstances. The trigger is in a country scope.
#
# division_types - is a list of tokens to corresponding unit types. A player can in fact use any group of names for a div.template
#                  however this tag is a helper for an automated choice (for AI, or if the group must switch on it's own, because
#                  for example the current one is no longer available due to the can_use trigger saying so).
#                  In automated choice, the division template must have at least 1 of the following types for it to be chosen.
#
# fallback_name - Is going to be used if we run out of the scripted historical names. If you want to use the old division naming
#                 mechanics to be used for fallbacks, then just skip this option.
#
# unordered - It's a list of historical division names that did not have a number. Regardless if such names happened in history or not
#             this option is available here mainly for a mods.
#
# ordered - Is a list of all historical names. 
#           Numbers must start from 1 and up. 
#           Numbers can't repeat in one scope.
#           If you script the name for this group, at the same number (for example in a mod in another file), the name will be override.
#           All arguments between the brackets must be separated by spaces. Each argument is wrapped in "quotas".
#           1st argument = The name. It must contain either: 
#                          %d (for decimal number placement)
#                          %s (for string number placement - ROMAN numbers like XIV).
#           2nd argument is optional = A localizable text describing this historical division. The text will be visible in the tooltip
#                                      where you choose the historical division name.
#           3rd argument is optional = An URL preferably pointing to the WIKI. It's a future feature that is not currently working in
#                                      the current game version.

GER_INF_01 = 
{
	name = "Infantry Divisions"

	for_countries = { GER }

	can_use = { 
		OR = { 
			has_start_date > 1935.10.01
			has_completed_focus = GER_Establish_the_Wehrmacht
		}	
	} 

	division_types = { "infantry" }

	# Number reservation system will tie to another group.
	link_numbering_with = { GER_INF_03 GER_HVY_01 GER_HVY_02 GER_LGH_01 GER_LGH_02 GER_MOT_01 GER_MEC_01 GER_GAR_01 GER_PAR_01 GER_PAR_02 GER_CRO_01 }

GER_INF_02 = 
{
	name = "General Divisions"	# Once you form the Reichswehr and start the rearmament process, this list will go away and you will switch to the cover names for the expansion.

	for_countries = { GER }

	can_use = { 
		has_start_date < 1935.10.1
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = GER_Reichswehr }
	} 

	division_types = { "infantry" }

	# Number reservation system will tie to another group.
	link_numbering_with = { GER_INF_03 }

	fallback_name = "%d. Division"

					has_completed_focus = GER_Luftwaffe

				casualties > 750000  # Will only see these units once the Heer takes a bunch of casualties.  Ballpark around how many casualties the Heer had taken when the Luftwaffe divisions were actually authorized.

GER_LGH_01 =

	name = "Light Infantry Divisions"

	for_countries = { GER }

	can_use = {
		has_start_date < 1942.07.06
		has_completed_focus = GER_Heer
		NOT = { 
			has_completed_focus = GER_Panzergrenadiers
			has_completed_focus = GER_Panzerkorps
		}	
	}

	division_types = { "light_infantry" }

GER_LGH_02 = 
{
	name = "Light Infantry Divisions"

	for_countries = { GER }

	can_use = { 
		OR = { 
			has_start_date > 1942.07.05
			has_completed_focus = GER_Panzergrenadiers
			has_completed_focus = GER_Panzerkorps
		}	
	} 

	division_types = { "light_infantry" }

	fallback_name = "%d. Jäger-Division"

	# Number reservation system will tie to another group.
	link_numbering_with = { GER_INF_01 GER_INF_03 GER_HVY_01 GER_HVY_02 GER_LGH_01 GER_MOT_01 GER_MEC_01 GER_GAR_01 GER_PAR_01 GER_PAR_02 GER_CRO_01 }

	# Names with numbers (only one number per entry)
	ordered =
	{
		8 = { "%d. Jäger-Division" }	# 34 10
		5 = { "%d. Jäger-Division" }	# 34 10
		28 = { "%d. Jäger-Division" }	# 36 10

		100 = { "%d. Jäger-Division" }	# 40 10

GER_MOT_01 = 
{
	name = "Motorized Divisions"

	for_countries = { GER }

	can_use = {
		OR = { 
			has_start_date > 1937.01.01
			has_completed_focus = GER_Establish_the_Wehrmacht
		}	
		NOT = { 
			OR = {
				has_start_date > 1943.06.22
				has_completed_focus = GER_Panzergrenadiers
				has_completed_focus = GER_Panzerkorps
			}
		}	
	}

	division_types = { "motorized" }

GER_MAR_01 = 
{
	name = "Marine Divisions"

	for_countries = { GER }

	can_use = { 
		OR = { 
			has_start_date > 1935.10.01
			has_completed_focus = GER_Reichsmarine
		}	
	} 

	division_types = { "marine" }

	fallback_name = "%d. Seelande-Division"

	# Names with numbers (only one number per entry)
	ordered =
	{
		1 = { "%d. Seelande-Division" }
		2 = { "%d. Seelande-Division" }
		3 = { "%d. Seelande-Division" }
		4 = { "%d. Seelande-Division" }
		5 = { "%d. Seelande-Division" }
		
		# chose to remove the old name list entirely as it refers to late war improvised infantry units built from idle naval personnel, with little in the way of ground combat training. These in no way constitute a naval assault landing unit which is what Marines are, so in the ahistorical event that the player chooses to invest in a proper German Marine Corps, we gave them the name of "Sea Landing Division" to more correctly reflect the role. This frees up the KM infantry divisions for the normal infantry name list.
	}
}

GER_PAR_01 = 
{
	name = "Paratrooper Divisions"

	for_countries = { GER }

	can_use = {
			has_start_date < 1943.05.01
			has_completed_focus = GER_Luftwaffe
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = GER_Fallschirmtruppen	}	
	}

	division_types = { "paratrooper" }

	fallback_name = "%d. Flieger-Division"

	# Number reservation system will tie to another group.
	link_numbering_with = { GER_INF_03 GER_HVY_01 GER_HVY_02 GER_LGH_01 GER_LGH_02 GER_MOT_01 GER_MEC_01 GER_GAR_01 GER_INF_01 GER_PAR_02 GER_CRO_01 }

	# Names with numbers (only one number per entry)
	ordered =
	{
		22 = { "%d. (Luftlande-)Infanterie-Division" } # 34 10
		501 = { "7. Flieger-Division" } # 38 09
		91 = { "%d. (Luftlande-)Infanterie-Division" } # 44 01 344. Infantry
		502 = { "2. Flieger-Division" } # The odd numbering is because the (LL) Inf.Div. have to link with the regular Infantry lists.  So all the Fallschirmjäger divisions get a blank spot in the number scheme.
		503 = { "3. Flieger-Division" }
		504 = { "4. Flieger-Division" }
		505 = { "5. Flieger-Division" }
		506 = { "6. Flieger-Division" }
		508 = { "8. Flieger-Division" }
		509 = { "9. Flieger-Division" }
		510 = { "10. Flieger-Division" }
		511 = { "11. Flieger-Division" }
		520 = { "20. Flieger-Division" }
		521 = { "21. Flieger-Division" }
		512 = { "12. Flieger-Division" } # Fictional from here.
		513 = { "13. Flieger-Division" }
		514 = { "14. Flieger-Division" }
		515 = { "15. Flieger-Division" }
		516 = { "16. Flieger-Division" }
		517 = { "17. Flieger-Division" }
		518 = { "18. Flieger-Division" }
		519 = { "19. Flieger-Division" }
		507 = { "1. Flieger-Division" } # Put way down here so you should never see this and to avoid conflict with 7. Flieger-Div.
		
		# I know that 22. (LL)Inf.Div. and 91. (LL)Inf.Div. weren't fully airborne units.  They had a mix of gliderborne forces and elements optimised for rapid air transport into newly captured airfields.
		# But they are included here because they are at least as airborne as most of the later Fallschirmjäger divisions which had no airborne training whatsoever.
		# This uses the early names for the Luftwaffe airborne divisions.  In reality only 7. Flieger-Div. was so named, but this way you get names that make sense if your ingame Germans manage to build more than three paratrooper divisions before taking the focus.
		# That's another reason why I included the (LL)Inf.Div. here.  You have more of a buffer before you get to ahistorical names.
	}
}

##		155 = { "%d. Feldausbildungs-Division" }
##		950 = { "Festungs-Division Danzig" }
##		951 = { "Festungs-Division Frankfurt/Oder" }
##		952 = { "Festungs-Division Gotenhafen" }

		# put in a large amount of assorted reserve, replacement, and training units if a meaningful history of antipartisan/frontline service could be attributed to them
		# included some of the Division z.b.V. ("for special use") that have a recorded service history in occupied territory. Most of these were ad hoc grouping of training/Landesschützen units inside Germany.
		# gave some reserve units a static name and linked them with a number in the infantry list as they were later upgraded to full infantry/Jäger divisions
		# deleted some reserve and training units only used as holding depots for recruits, etc.
		# 153. Reserve Division only went by this name for a few months while forming, so went with 153. Feldausbildungs-Division as this was the name it saw out the majority of its life as.
		# removed Volksgrenadiers from this list as they were not static defense units, rather late war normal infantry divisions organized on a 'many weapons - few men' basis. Put them in the Alt Infantry list.
	}
}

GER_ARM_01 = 
{
	name = "Armored Divisions"

	for_countries = { GER }

	can_use = {
		OR = { 
			has_start_date > 1935.01.01
			has_completed_focus = GER_Establish_the_Wehrmacht
		}	
	}

	division_types = { "light_armor" "medium_armor" "heavy_armor" }

	fallback_name = "%d. Panzer-Division"

	link_numbering_with = { GER_LARM_01 GER_ART_01 }

	# Names with numbers (only one number per entry)
	ordered =
	{

		7 = { "%d. Panzer-Division" } #1939 10
		9 = { "%d. Panzer-Division" } #1940 03

		14 = { "%d. Panzer-Division" } #1940 08
		12 = { "%d. Panzer-Division" } #1940 10
		13 = { "Panzer-Division „Feldherrnhalle 2“" } #1940 10
		20 = { "%d. Panzer-Division" } #1940 10

		15 = { "%d. Panzer-Division" } #1940 11

		25 = { "%d. Panzer-Division" } #1942 02
		26 = { "%d. Panzer-Division" } #1942 09
		27 = { "%d. Panzer-Division" } #1942 10
		693 = { "Fallschirm-Panzer-Division 1 „Hermann Göring“" } #1942 11
		85 = { "Panzer-Division „Clausewitz“" } #1943 04
		130 = { "Panzer-Lehr-Division" } #1944 01
		116 = { "%d. Panzer-Division" } #1944 03
		60 = { "Panzer-Division „Feldherrnhalle“" } #1944 10
		232 = { "%d. Panzer-Division" } #1945 02
		233 = { "Panzer-Division „Holstein“" } #1945 02
		88 = { "Panzer-Division „Müncheberg“" } #1945 03
		28 = { "%d. Panzer-Division" } #Fictinal for numbering purposes
	
		# deleted Panzer-Division 'Kurmark' because it is actually just an erroneous name for PzG Div Kurmark in some postwar literature
		# deleted Panzer-Division 'Kempf' as it was a temporary adhoc grouping of army tanks and SS infantry for the Polish campaign, which was quickly broken up after and absorbed by 10. Panzer-Division
		# deleted Panzer-Division Tatra as it was only used as a security/holding unit, and then renamed to 232. Panzer-Division which did in fact see active combat
		# deleted Panzer-Divisions Jüterbog and Schlesien as they was used as a holding unit and disbanded a month after formation
		# deleted Norwegen Panzer Division as Norway is not guaranteed to be occupied by Germany in every game, plus it was in reality no more than a brigade in size despite the title.
		# had to settle on a single name for the HG Panzer Division despite several historical name changes over time
		# no way to register things like 1. Kavallerie-Division becoming 24. Panzer, 13. Panzer becoming Feldherrnhalle 2, etc, without bloating the name list selection and causing obnoxious clutter. The ability to rename is there though, for those who are really devoted.
		# deleted most of the Reserve-Panzer-Divisions because they were holding units for recruits, and quickly disbanded after being used to replenish field units

	}
}

GER_LARM_01 = 
{
	name = "Light Armored Divisions"

	for_countries = { GER }

	can_use = {
		OR = { 
			has_start_date > 1935.01.01
			has_completed_focus = GER_Establish_the_Wehrmacht
		}	
	}

	division_types = { "light_armor" }

	fallback_name = "%d. leichte-Division"
	
	link_numbering_with = { GER_ARM_01 GER_ART_01 }

	# Names with numbers (only one number per entry)
	ordered =
	{
	9 = { "4. leichte-Division" }
	6 = { "1. leichte-Division" }
	7 = { "2. leichte-Division" }
	8 = { "3. leichte-Division" }
	21 = { "5. leichte-Division" }
	
	# a small series of early war 'light' armoured divisions raised as an attempt by the cavalry branch to remain relevant in modern war. They were found to be too light to fight after Poland and converted in to full Panzer Divisions. X = number of the Panzer Division they were converted in to.
	
	}
}

		46 = { "%d. SS-Division „Der Führer“" } #Austria. Thought it would be appropriate to have this name for a division from Hitler's home.
		47 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Division „De Ruiter“" } #Netherlands
		48 = { "%d. Division der SS „Miloš Obilić“ (serbisch Nr. 1)" }  #Serbia
		49 = { "%d. SS-Division „Kurt Eggers“" }  # The SS war correspondent regiment was named after Eggers.
		50 = { "%d. Division der SS „Tigerlegion“ (indisch Nr. 1)" }  #India. There actually was a Tiger Legion under SS control made up of Indians taken as POWs from British units.  No reason the Legion couldn't be expanded to a division following a German occupation of India.
		51 = { "%d. Division der SS „Voldemārs Veiss“ (lettische Nr. 3)" } #Latvia
		52 = { "%d. SS-Division „Hermann von Salza“" }

		54 = { "%d. SS-Division „Wallenstein“" }  # Czech
		55 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Division „Wilhelm Gustloff“ (schweizerisch Nr.1)" } #Switzerland
		56 = { "%d. Division der SS (französische Nr. 2)" }  #France
		57 = { "%d. SS-Division „Germania“" }  #
		58 = { "%d. Division der SS „Wilhelm der Eroberer“ (englisch Nr. 1)" }  #England
		59 = { "%d. Division der SS „Owain Glyndŵr“ (walisisch Nr. 1)" }  #Wales. Germany actually had a seaplane carrier during the First World War called Glyndwr.
		60 = { "%d. Division der SS „Claymore“ (schottisch Nr. 1)" }  #Scotland.  Following the scheme of naming SS Division after local sword or fighting knife.
		61 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Division „Beowulf“ (englisch Nr. 2)" } #England
		62 = { "%d. Division der SS „Fionn mac Cumhaill“ (irländisch Nr. 1)" }  #Ireland
		63 = { "%d. SS-Division „Reinhard Heydrich“" }
		64 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Division „Paul Kruger“ (burisch Nr. 1)" } #South Africa
		65 = { "%d. SS-Division „Thule“" }


		# to avoid massively bloating the names list with alternate lists, the final/most representative divisional name was used. Das Reich held no less than 6 different names during the war and providing variant name lists for all of them was not feasible. The tools to rename/reconfigure divisions are in the hands of the player, however.
		# left out divisional type names (Panzer, Gebirgs, etc) to allow the player to use the SS name list for any type of division they choose
		# diverged from the ordering based on historical formation date as this to a large degree would depend on the divisional type, which is not fixed
		# put in non-German formations contrary to the regular Heer lists
	}
}

		50 = { "%d. Waffen-Grenadier-Division der SS „Tigerlegion“ (indisch Nr. 1)" }  #India. There actually was a Tiger Legion under SS control made up of Indians taken as POWs from British units.  No reason the Legion couldn't be expanded to a division following a German occupation of India.
		51 = { "%d. Waffen-Grenadier-Division der SS „Voldemārs Veiss“ (lettische Nr. 3)" } #Latvia
		52 = { "%d. SS-Grenadier-Division „Hermann von Salza“" }
		53 = { "%d. Waffen-Grenadier-Division der SS „Ustym Karmaliuk“ (galizische Nr. 2)" } #Ukraine
		54 = { "%d. SS-Grenadier-Division „Wallenstein“" }  # Czech
		55 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Grenadier-Division „Wilhelm Gustloff“ (schweizerisch Nr.1)" } #Switzerland
		56 = { "%d. Waffen-Grenadier-Division der SS (französische Nr. 2)" }  #France
		57 = { "%d. SS-Grenadier-Division „Germania“" }  #
		58 = { "%d. Waffen-Grenadier-Division der SS „Wilhelm der Eroberer“ (englisch Nr. 1)" }  #England
		59 = { "%d. Waffen-Grenadier-Division der SS „Owain Glyndŵr“ (walisisch Nr. 1)" }  #Wales. Germany actually had a seaplane carrier during the First World War called Glyndwr.
		60 = { "%d. Waffen-Grenadier-Division der SS „Claymore“ (schottisch Nr. 1)" }  #Scotland.  Following the scheme of naming SS Division after local sword or fighting knife.
		61 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Grenadier-Division „Beowulf“ (englisch Nr. 2)" } #England
		62 = { "%d. Waffen-Grenadier-Division der SS „Fionn mac Cumhaill“ (irländisch Nr. 1)" }  #Ireland
		63 = { "%d. SS-Grenadier-Division „Reinhard Heydrich“" }
		64 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Grenadier-Division „Paul Kruger“ (burisch Nr. 1)" } #South Africa
		65 = { "%d. SS-Grenadier-Division „Thule“" }


		# to avoid massively bloating the names list with alternate lists, the final/most representative divisional name was used. Das Reich held no less than 6 different names during the war and providing variant name lists for all of them was not feasible. The tools to rename/reconfigure divisions are in the hands of the player, however.
		# left out divisional type names (Panzer, Gebirgs, etc) to allow the player to use the SS name list for any type of division they choose
		# diverged from the ordering based on historical formation date as this to a large degree would depend on the divisional type, which is not fixed
		# put in non-German formations contrary to the regular Heer lists
	}
}
GER_SS_CAV_01 = 
{
	name = "SS Cavalry Divisions"

	for_countries = { GER }

	can_use = { 
		has_government = fascist
		has_completed_focus = GER_Waffen_SS
	}

	division_types = { "SS_cavalry" }

	fallback_name = "%d. SS-Kavallerie-Division"

	link_numbering_with = { GER_SS_02 GER_SS_01 GER_SS_INF_01 GER_SS_MEC_01 GER_SS_ARM_01 GER_SS_MTN_01 }

	# Names with numbers (only one number per entry)
	ordered =
	{
		1 = { "%d. SS-Kavallerie-Division „Leibstandarte SS Adolf Hitler“" }
		2 = { "%d. SS-Kavallerie-Division „Das Reich“" }
		3 = { "%d. SS-Kavallerie-Division „Totenkopf“" } #Concentration camp guards equipped with captured Czech equipment
		4 = { "%d. SS-Polizei-Kavallerie-Division" } # Police officers.  Captured Czech equipmment.
		5 = { "%d. SS-Kavallerie-Division „Wiking“" }  #Scandinavia
		6 = { "%d. SS-Kavallerie-Division „Nord“" }  #Mountain Division
		7 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Kavallerie-Division „Prinz Eugen“" }  #Mountain Division.  Banat, Croatia, Hungary, Romania
		8 = { "%d. SS-Kavallerie-Division „Florian Geyer“" }  #Cavalry Division
		9 = { "%d. SS-Kavallerie-Division „Hohenstaufen“" }
		10 = { "%d. SS-Kavallerie-Division „Frundsberg“" }
		11 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Kavallerie-Division „Nordland“" }
		12 = { "%d. SS-Kavallerie-Division „Hitlerjugend“" }
		13 = { "%d. Waffen-Kavallerie-Division der SS „Handschar“ (kroatische Nr. 1)" }  #Mountain Division.
		14 = { "%d. Waffen-Kavallerie-Division der SS (galizische Nr. 1)" }
		15 = { "%d. Waffen-Kavallerie-Division der SS (lettische Nr. 1)" }
		16 = { "%d. SS-Kavallerie-Division „Reichsführer-SS“" }
		17 = { "%d. SS-Kavallerie-Division „Götz von Berlichingen“" }
		18 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Kavallerie-Division „Horst Wessel“" }
		19 = { "%d. Waffen-Kavallerie-Division der SS (lettische Nr. 2)" }
		20 = { "%d. Waffen-Kavallerie-Division der SS (estnische Nr. 1)" }
		21 = { "%d. Waffen-Kavallerie-Division der SS „Skanderbeg“ (albanische Nr.1)" }  #Mountain Division.
		22 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Kavallerie-Division „Maria Theresia“" }  #Cavalry Division. The name Maria Theresia may not have been given to the unit at the time.  But isnce it is widely referred to as such, I'm keeping it.
		23 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Kavallerie-Division „Nederland“ (Niederländische Nr. 1)" } # This was a tough one.  There was also the 23. Division der SS 'Kama' (Kroatische Nr. 2) but that organization never fought as a unit and actually mutinied against their German leadership.  The Netherland division had 3 times the manpower.
		24 = { "%d. Waffen-Kavallerie-Division der SS „Karstjäger“" }  #Mountain Division.
		25 = { "%d. Waffen-Kavallerie-Division der SS „Hunyadi“ (ungarische Nr. 1)" }
		26 = { "%d. Waffen-Kavallerie-Division der SS (ungarische Nr. 2)" }
		27 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Kavallerie-Division „Langemarck“ (flämische Nr. 1)" }
		28 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Kavallerie-Division „Wallonien“" }
		29 = { "%d. Waffen-Kavallerie-Division der SS (italienische Nr. 1)" } # There was also the 29th Russian SS Division, but it was just the Kaminski Brigade received orders to expand to a division and those orders were rescinded within a month as a result of their performance during the Warsaw Uprising.  The RONA units worth keeping were then reorganized into Wehrmacht units.
		30 = { "%d. Waffen-Kavallerie-Division der SS (weißruthenische Nr. 1)" }
		31 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Kavallerie-Division „Batschka“" }
		32 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Kavallerie-Division „30. Januar“" }
		33 = { "%d. Waffen-Kavallerie-Division der SS „Charlemagne“ (französische Nr. 1)" } # The number 33 originally went to a third Hungarian SS division, but that 'division' only briefly had a single regiment.  The Charlemagne division is far more historically significant.
		34 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Kavallerie-Division „Landstorm Nederland“" }
		35 = { "%d. SS und Polizei-Division" }
		36 = { "%d. Waffen-Kavallerie-Division der SS „Dirlewanger“" }
		37 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Kavallerie-Division „Lützow“" }  #Cavalry Division
		38 = { "%d. SS-Kavallerie-Division „Nibelungen“" }
		39 = { "%d. SS-Kavallerie-Division „Waräger“" }  #fictional units start here
		40 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Kavallerie-Division „Kalevala“" } #Finland.  The Finnish national epic. Also cited in several sources as the planned name of a Finnish SS Division.
		41 = { "%d. Waffen-Kavallerie-Division der SS „Vendetta“ (italienische Nr. 2)" }
		42 = { "%d. Waffen-Kavallerie-Division der SS „Hlinka-Garde“ (slowakisch Nr.1)" } #Slovakia. After the Slovak National Uprising, the Hlinka Guard did come under the authority of the German SS, but it was never formally organized into a SS unit.
		43 = { "%d. SS-Kavallerie-Division „Theodor Eicke“" }  # Possibly another Totenkopf division but would work for any German SS.
		44 = { "%d. SS-Kavallerie-Division „Herbert Norkus“" }  #Hitler Youth 2.  Norkus was a Hitler Youth martyr
		45 = { "%d. SS-Kavallerie-Division „Andreas Hofer“" } #Austria. Hofer was an 18th century folk hero and freedom fighter.
		46 = { "%d. SS-Kavallerie-Division „Der Führer“" } #Austria. Thought it would be appropriate to have this name for a division from Hitler's home.
		47 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Kavallerie-Division „De Ruiter“" } #Netherlands
		48 = { "%d. Waffen-Kavallerie-Division der SS „Miloš Obilić“ (serbisch Nr. 1)" }  #Serbia
		49 = { "%d. SS-Kavallerie-Division „Kurt Eggers“" }  # The SS war correspondent regiment was named after Eggers.
		50 = { "%d. Waffen-Kavallerie-Division der SS „Tigerlegion“ (indisch Nr. 1)" }  #India. There actually was a Tiger Legion under SS control made up of Indians taken as POWs from British units.  No reason the Legion couldn't be expanded to a division following a German occupation of India.
		51 = { "%d. Waffen-Kavallerie-Division der SS „Voldemārs Veiss“ (lettische Nr. 3)" } #Latvia
		52 = { "%d. SS-Kavallerie-Division „Hermann von Salza“" }
		53 = { "%d. Waffen-Kavallerie-Division der SS „Ustym Karmaliuk“ (galizische Nr. 2)" } #Ukraine
		54 = { "%d. SS-Kavallerie-Division „Wallenstein“" }  # Czech
		55 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Kavallerie-Division „Wilhelm Gustloff“ (schweizerisch Nr.1)" } #Switzerland
		56 = { "%d. Waffen-Kavallerie-Division der SS (französische Nr. 2)" }  #France
		57 = { "%d. SS-Kavallerie-Division „Germania“" }  #
		58 = { "%d. Waffen-Kavallerie-Division der SS „Wilhelm der Eroberer“ (englisch Nr. 1)" }  #England
		59 = { "%d. Waffen-Kavallerie-Division der SS „Owain Glyndŵr“ (walisisch Nr. 1)" }  #Wales. Germany actually had a seaplane carrier during the First World War called Glyndwr.
		60 = { "%d. Waffen-Kavallerie-Division der SS „Claymore“ (schottisch Nr. 1)" }  #Scotland.  Following the scheme of naming SS Division after local sword or fighting knife.
		61 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Kavallerie-Division „Beowulf“ (englisch Nr. 2)" } #England
		62 = { "%d. Waffen-Kavallerie-Division der SS „Fionn mac Cumhaill“ (irländisch Nr. 1)" }  #Ireland
		63 = { "%d. SS-Kavallerie-Division „Reinhard Heydrich“" }
		64 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Kavallerie-Division „Paul Kruger“ (burisch Nr. 1)" } #South Africa
		65 = { "%d. SS-Kavallerie-Division „Thule“" }


		# to avoid massively bloating the names list with alternate lists, the final/most representative divisional name was used. Das Reich held no less than 6 different names during the war and providing variant name lists for all of them was not feasible. The tools to rename/reconfigure divisions are in the hands of the player, however.
		# left out divisional type names (Panzer, Gebirgs, etc) to allow the player to use the SS name list for any type of division they choose
		# diverged from the ordering based on historical formation date as this to a large degree would depend on the divisional type, which is not fixed
		# put in non-German formations contrary to the regular Heer lists
	}

		25 = { "%d. Waffen-Panzer-Division der SS „Hunyadi“ (ungarische Nr. 1)" }
		26 = { "%d. Waffen-Panzer-Division der SS (ungarische Nr. 2)" }
		27 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Panzer-Division „Langemarck“ (flämische Nr. 1)" }
		28 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Panzer-Division „Wallonien“" }
		29 = { "%d. Waffen-Panzer-Division der SS (italienische Nr. 1)" } # There was also the 29th Russian SS Division, but it was just the Kaminski Brigade received orders to expand to a division and those orders were rescinded within a month as a result of their performance during the Warsaw Uprising.  The RONA units worth keeping were then reorganized into Wehrmacht units.
		30 = { "%d. Waffen-Panzer-Division der SS (weißruthenische Nr. 1)" }
		31 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Panzer-Division „Batschka“" }
		32 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Panzer-Division „30. Januar“" }
		33 = { "%d. Waffen-Panzer-Division der SS „Charlemagne“ (französische Nr. 1)" } # The number 33 originally went to a third Hungarian SS division, but that 'division' only briefly had a single regiment.  The Charlemagne division is far more historically significant.
		34 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Panzer-Division „Landstorm Nederland“" }
		35 = { "%d. SS und Polizei-Division" }
		36 = { "%d. Waffen-Panzer-Division der SS „Dirlewanger“" }
		37 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Panzer-Division „Lützow“" }  #Cavalry Division
		38 = { "%d. SS-Panzer-Division „Nibelungen“" }
		39 = { "%d. SS-Panzer-Division „Waräger“" }  #fictional units start here
		40 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Panzer-Division „Kalevala“" } #Finland.  The Finnish national epic. Also cited in several sources as the planned name of a Finnish SS Division.
		41 = { "%d. Waffen-Panzer-Division der SS „Vendetta“ (italienische Nr. 2)" }
		42 = { "%d. Waffen-Panzer-Division der SS „Hlinka-Garde“ (slowakisch Nr.1)" } #Slovakia. After the Slovak National Uprising, the Hlinka Guard did come under the authority of the German SS, but it was never formally organized into a SS unit.
		43 = { "%d. SS-Panzer-Division „Theodor Eicke“" }  # Possibly another Totenkopf division but would work for any German SS.
		44 = { "%d. SS-Panzer-Division „Herbert Norkus“" }  #Hitler Youth 2.  Norkus was a Hitler Youth martyr
		45 = { "%d. SS-Panzer-Division „Andreas Hofer“" } #Austria. Hofer was an 18th century folk hero and freedom fighter.
		46 = { "%d. SS-Panzer-Division „Der Führer“" } #Austria. Thought it would be appropriate to have this name for a division from Hitler's home.
		47 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Panzer-Division „De Ruiter“" } #Netherlands
		48 = { "%d. Waffen-Panzer-Division der SS „Miloš Obilić“ (serbisch Nr. 1)" }  #Serbia
		49 = { "%d. SS-Panzer-Division „Kurt Eggers“" }  # The SS war correspondent regiment was named after Eggers.
		50 = { "%d. Waffen-Panzer-Division der SS „Tigerlegion“ (indisch Nr. 1)" }  #India. There actually was a Tiger Legion under SS control made up of Indians taken as POWs from British units.  No reason the Legion couldn't be expanded to a division following a German occupation of India.
		51 = { "%d. Waffen-Panzer-Division der SS „Voldemārs Veiss“ (lettische Nr. 3)" } #Latvia
		52 = { "%d. SS-Panzer-Division „Hermann von Salza“" }
		53 = { "%d. Waffen-Panzer-Division der SS „Ustym Karmaliuk“ (galizische Nr. 2)" } #Ukraine
		54 = { "%d. SS-Panzer-Division „Wallenstein“" }  # Czech
		55 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Panzer-Division „Wilhelm Gustloff“ (schweizerisch Nr.1)" } #Switzerland
		56 = { "%d. Waffen-Panzer-Division der SS (französische Nr. 2)" }  #France
		57 = { "%d. SS-Panzer-Division „Germania“" }  #
		58 = { "%d. Waffen-Panzer-Division der SS „Wilhelm der Eroberer“ (englisch Nr. 1)" }  #England
		59 = { "%d. Waffen-Panzer-Division der SS „Owain Glyndŵr“ (walisisch Nr. 1)" }  #Wales. Germany actually had a seaplane carrier during the First World War called Glyndwr.
		60 = { "%d. Waffen-Panzer-Division der SS „Claymore“ (schottisch Nr. 1)" }  #Scotland.  Following the scheme of naming SS Division after local sword or fighting knife.
		61 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Panzer-Division „Beowulf“ (englisch Nr. 2)" } #England
		62 = { "%d. Waffen-Panzer-Division der SS „Fionn mac Cumhaill“ (irländisch Nr. 1)" }  #Ireland
		63 = { "%d. SS-Panzer-Division „Reinhard Heydrich“" }
		64 = { "%d. SS-Freiwilligen-Panzer-Division „Paul Kruger“ (burisch Nr. 1)" } #South Africa
		65 = { "%d. SS-Panzer-Division „Thule“" }


		# to avoid massively bloating the names list with alternate lists, the final/most representative divisional name was used. Das Reich held no less than 6 different names during the war and providing variant name lists for all of them was not feasible. The tools to rename/reconfigure divisions are in the hands of the player, however.
		# left out divisional type names (Panzer, Gebirgs, etc) to allow the player to use the SS name list for any type of division they choose
		# diverged from the ordering based on historical formation date as this to a large degree would depend on the divisional type, which is not fixed
		# put in non-German formations contrary to the regular Heer lists
	}
}

GER_SSCav_01 = 
{
	name = "Cossack Divisions"

	for_countries = { GER }

	can_use = { 
		has_government = fascist
		has_completed_focus = GER_SS_Freiwillige_Divisions
		OR = { 
			has_war_with = SOV
			is_in_faction_with = RUK
			is_in_faction_with = UKR
			is_in_faction_with = RKA
			controls_state = 218
			controls_state = 217
			controls_state = 234
			controls_state = 232
		}
	}

	division_types = { "SS_cavalry" }

	fallback_name = "%d. Kosaken-Kavallerie-Division"

	# Names with numbers (only one number per entry)
	ordered =
	{
		1 = { "%d. Kosaken-Kavallerie-Division" }
		2 = { "%d. Kosaken-Kavallerie-Division" }
		3 = { "%d. Kosaken-Plastun-Division" }  # Plastun was actually Cossack infantry.  Germany had a plan to turn the Plastun Brigade into a full division
		4 = { "%d. Don-Kosaken-Kavallerie-Division" } # The Cossack hosts had their own Brigades within the divisions.  If the war had gone on, it is reasonable to think these Brigades would be reorganized in this fashion.
		5 = { "%d. Kuban-Kosaken-Kavallerie-Division" }
		6 = { "%d. Kosaken-Plastun-Division" }
		7 = { "%d. Sibirisches-Kosaken-Kavallerie-Division" }
		8 = { "%d. Terek-Kosaken-Kavallerie-Division" }
		9 = { "%d. Kosaken-Plastun-Division" }
	}
	
}
